## grow SDSSDA240G
su > "root" pw   dhcpcd enp0s8   ping -c 3 8.8.8.8  got a response   pacman -S parted
lsblk  indicated  parted /dev/sdb > [ print  reports  4  ends at 206GB
  but  resizepart 4 230GiB  gets "outside of the device /dev/sdb" ] so:
    resizepart 4 100%  gets  End 240GB   resizepart 4 230GB > Yes
    sfdisk /dev/sdb -l  doesn't tell me the size of the ext4, and no way, apparently
pacman -S gparted  = 7 packages
  sudo gparted  shows visually that the filesystem ain't filling the partition,
    but no means to non-destructively change that...
resize2fs /dev/sdb4  "The filesystem on /dev/sdb4 is now 34136087 (4k) blocks long."
  sudo gparted  visually confirms that it's fully populated
dumpe2fs -h /dev/sdb4  confirms the block count
